Here is a sample stress-at-work questionnaire:

**Stress At Work Questionnaire**

The purpose of this survey is to understand how you experience and manage workplace-related stresses, as well as identify potential areas for improvement. Your responses will be kept confidential.

1. **Frequency Of Feeling Stressed**
How often do you feel stressed at work?

a) Almost never
b) Rarely (about once a month)
c) Sometimes (every few weeks or so)

2. **Causes of Stress**

Which, if any, factors contribute to your stress levels? Please select all that apply:

* Unrealistic workload and deadlines 
* Lack of control over work tasks  
* Conflicting priorities   
* Unclear expectations from management
* Poor communication with colleagues/team members    
Other (please specify): _______________________

3. **Impact On Well-being**

How do you think workplace stress affects your overall well-being?

a) It has a significant negative impact on my mental and physical health.
b) Stress at work can be challenging, but I manage to cope relatively effectively.

4. **Coping Mechanisms**
What strategies or habits help reduce the effects of job-related stresses? Please select all that apply:

* Taking regular breaks
* Prioritizing tasks more efficiently 
* Seeking support from colleagues/friends/ family members    
Practicing mindfulness/meditation   
Engaging in physical activity/exercise outside work hours  
Other (please specify): _______________________

5. **Managerial Support**
Do you feel like your manager or supervisor:

a) Provides adequate emotional and practical help when needed
b) Is somewhat supportive, but could do better

6. **Work-Life Balance**

How would rate the balance between personal life outside work hours?

* Excellent (I have a healthy separation)
* Good 
Fairly poor   
Poor 

7.**Suggestions For Improvement**
What changes or initiatives might you suggest to reduce workplace stress? Please provide any additional comments:

______________________________________________________________________
Thank You for taking time to share your thoughts and experiences!

[LLM ANSWER]
Here's a sample questionnaire for investigating workplace environment:

**Workplace Environmental Survey**

As we strive to create an optimal work atmosphere, I'd like you take this opportunity to share your thoughts and opinions about our current workspace. Your input will help us identify areas of improvement.

Please answer the questions honestly; all responses are anonymous unless otherwise specified (indicated by *).

1.* What is most important aspect for a comfortable workplace environment in my opinion?

a) Natural Light
b) Temperature Control 
c* Noise Level Management  
d*) Collaborative Spaces

2. How would you rate your overall satisfaction with the current workspace? 

(Scale: 5 - Very Satisfied, to 1- Not at All)

3.* What do I like most about our workplace environment?

(Open-ended text response)
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Workplace Environment

```
{

              {"ANSWER": "3 - Neutral"},

              {"ANSWER": "1 - Not at All"}

[LLM ANSWER]
Here's a sample questionnaire for gathering information related to remote work experiences:

**Remote Working Experience Questionnaire**

As part of our ongoing efforts to improve and adapt to changing workplace dynamics, we're interested in hearing about your personal experiences with remote or flexible work arrangements. Your input will help us better understand the benefits, challenges, and best practices associated with working remotely.

Please answer these questions honestly based on your current (or most recent) experience:

**Section 1: General Information**

* What is/was your role when you worked from home/remotely? _______________________________________________________
	+ Full-time employee
    + Part-time or freelance worker

How often did/do you work remotely?

   * Daily 
     Weekly  
       Occasionally (please specify) _______________________________

**Section 2: Productivity and Focus**

1. How would rate your overall productivity while working from home/remotely? 

(Scale of 5, where:

    Very High
      Somewhat Higher than usual    
        About the same as when I work in-office   
          Less productive

Please explain any differences you've noticed.

2. What are some strategies or tools that help/have helped maintain your focus and concentration while working remotely? (Check all applicable)

   * Noise-cancelling headphones
     Music/white noise apps 
       Pomodoro timer techniques    
         Other: _______________________________________________________

**Section 3: Communication**

1. How do you currently communicate with colleagues, managers, or clients when not physically present in the office?

    Email and instant messaging platforms (e.g., Slack)
      Video conferencing tools like Zoom/Google Meet
        Phone calls/Skype 
          In-person meetings

2. Have there been any instances where communication challenges arose while working remotely? If yes:

   * Please describe: _______________________________________________________
     How did you resolve the issue?

**Section 4: Work-Life Balance**

1. Do/did remote work arrangements allow for a better balance between your professional and personal life?
    Yes
      No

2. What are some benefits or advantages of working remotely that have positively impacted other aspects (e.g., family, health) in addition to productivity?

**Section 5: Challenges & Suggestions**

1. Are there any specific challenges you've faced while remote-working? If yes:

   * Please describe the challenge and how it affected your work experience.
     How did/does management or colleagues support/help address this issue?
2. What suggestions do/did have for improving our company's approach to flexible working arrangements?

**Section 6: Additional Comments**

Is there anything else you'd like share about remote-working experiences, benefits, challenges, tips and tricks? _______________________________________________________

Thank You!

Please note that all responses will be kept confidential.

Let me know if this meets your requirements or need any modifications!

**End Of Working Relationship Questionnaire**

We value our employees' feedback and would like to understand your experience when an employment contract came to its natural conclusion. Your responses will help us improve the overall employee journey.

Please answer these questions honestly, considering only one instance of ending a working relationship with [Company Name].

1a) What was the reason for leaving/being let go (Select all that apply)?

* Voluntary resignation
* Involuntarily terminated by employer due to performance issues or misconduct
* Company restructuring/reduction in force
* Job elimination/duplicate role created within organization
* Other reasons, please specify: _______________________

1b) How would you rate your overall experience with the company during and after leaving?

(Scale of 5)

Not at all satisfied (1)
Somewhat dissatisfied (-2 to -3.9)
Neutral/No strong feelings (+0 or ±4-6%)
Slightly pleased (++7%+/-10%)

* Name: _____________________________________________________
* Job Title/Position:_____________________________________________

---

### Section 1 - Pre-Onboarding Experience

• I received clear information about what my role would entail. ____________________
	+ Strongly Agree
	+ Somewhat Agreed
	+ Neither agree nor disagree
	+ Somewhat disagreed
	+ Strongly disagrees

	+ Somewhat Agreed

    + Mostly clear.

### Section 5 - Additional Comments

_____________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________

Thank your participants and appreciate their time!

[LLM ANSWER]
Here's a sample questionnaire for gathering manager-level insights:

**Manager Feedback Questionnaire**

As part of our ongoing efforts to improve team performance and employee satisfaction, we value your input as managers. Your responses will help us identify areas where employees are excelling or struggling.

Please answer the following questions honestly based on recent experiences with direct reports (employees who report directly to you).

1.
What do YOU think is most important for an effective manager? Please rank in order of priority:

a) Clear communication
b) Setting achievable goals and objectives 
c) Providing constructive feedback & coaching

2. How would rate the overall performance management process within your team?

Scale:  (Excellent),   ,    or 

3.
What do you think is one area where we could improve our employee development programs? Please provide specific suggestions.

4. Have there been any instances recently when an underperforming direct report required additional support and guidance from HR/Management?
If yes, please describe the situation:

5. How often would YOU like to receive feedback on your own performance as a manager?

a) Quarterly
b) Semi-annually (every 6 months)
c) Annually

d) Other: _______________________________________

Please specify any additional comments or suggestions you may have for improving our employee development programs.

**Additional Comments/Suggestions:**


This questionnaire aims to gather insights on what managers think is most important, their experiences with performance management and feedback processes. It also touches upon areas where employees might need more support from HR/Management.


Let me know if this meets your expectations or would you like any changes!

**Career Path Questionnaire**

We're interested in understanding how employees perceive and navigate their careers at our company! Your input will help us identify trends, areas of improvement, and opportunities to support employee growth.

(Scale: Less than 6 months | Between 7-12 months | More than a year)

a. Frequently (at least once every quarter)
b. Occasionally, but not regularly
c. Rarely/Not really

(Select all that apply)

* New challenges and responsibilities 
* Increased salary or benefits package  
* Desire for more autonomy/independence   
Other (please specify): _______________________________________

a. Lack of opportunities
b. Limited growth prospects within the role/department

(Open-ended response)

**Benefits Perception Survey**

We value our employees' opinions! This survey aims at understanding how you perceive and utilize various company-provided benefits, helping us to refine or introduce new perks that meet your needs.

Please answer the questions honestly. Your input will be kept confidential!

1.

* Health insurance
* Retirement planning options 
* Paid time off/vacation days  
* Professional development opportunities   
Other: _______________________________________

2.

How satisfied are you with the current benefits package offered by our company?

a) Very Satisfied

b) Somewhat Satisfactory 

c) Neutral/Undecided  

d) Not very satisfying   

e) Extremely Dissatisified


3.
Which of these additional perks would YOU like to see introduced or improved? (Select all applicable)

* Flexible work arrangements 
* Employee discounts on company products/services
* On-site fitness classes/workshops  
* Mental health resources/support   
Other: _______________________________________

4.

Have you ever used any benefits provided by the organization?

a) Yes, I've utilized some of them

b) No/Not yet 

5.

6.

 a) Monthly
 b) Quarterly  
 c) Semiannually   
 d) Annually  

7.

a) Yes, I'd love the opportunity!

b) No/I'm not interested

8.
Any additional comments or suggestions about our current benefit offerings? (Open-ended response)

Thank YOU! Your input is invaluable in helping us create a more supportive and rewarding workplace environment.

**Career Development Questionnaire**

New challenges
Increased responsibility 
Career advancement opportunities

______________________________________________

_____________________________________________________________________

(Where: 
    - Not at all (0) to Very Satisfied)

6. What type(s) or training/development opportunities would be most valuable in helping achieve career goals?

Select one:

Mentorship
Workshops/Seminars

On-the-job learning/training 
Other (please specify): _______________________________________

Please describe the program(s) and your experience: ________________________________

**Section 4: Feedback & Support**

8. How often do you receive constructive feedback from supervisors/managers?

Rarely
Occasionally 
Regular

9a). Do feel supported in pursuing career goals within [Company Name]?
Yes, I have a clear understanding of what's expected.
Somewhat - there are some areas where support is lacking.

No/Not really 

**Section 5: Additional Comments**

10. Is there anything else you'd like to share about your current role or potential future opportunities for growth and development within [Company Name]?

_____________________________________________________________________

Thank You!

Please note that all responses will be kept confidential unless otherwise specified by the respondent (see instructions at end).

Here's a sample questionnaire for investigating career path clarity within an organization:

**Career Path Clarity Questionnaire**

As part of our ongoing efforts to support employee growth and development, we're interested in understanding your experiences with regards to having clear guidance about potential careers paths. Your input will help us identify areas where improvement is needed.

Please answer the following questions honestly based on what you know or have experienced:

**Section 1: Career Path Awareness**

1a) How often do I feel informed and aware of available career path options within my department/team?

(Scale: Very Often, Somewhat Frequently, Rarely)

b. Can you describe a specific instance where this awareness helped me make an important decision about your professional development? (Open-ended text field for respondents to share their experiences.)

**Section 2: Career Path Guidance**

1a) How confident do I feel that my supervisor/manager provides clear guidance on potential career paths and opportunities?

(Scale: Very Confident, Somewhat Confident, Not at All)

b. Have you ever received feedback or coaching from your manager/supervisor about how to advance in their role? If yes:

* What specific actions did they suggest?
	+ (Open-ended text field for respondents)
2a) How often do I feel that my organization provides opportunities and resources necessary for me to explore different career paths?

(Scale: Very Often, Somewhat Frequently, Rarely)

**Section 3: Career Path Development**

1. Have you ever taken a course or attended training sessions related specifically to your desired role? If yes:

* What was the topic of this learning experience?
	+ (Open-ended text field for respondents)
2a) How satisfied am I with my current job's alignment towards long-term career goals?

(Scale: Very Satisfied, Somewhat Satisfactionalized)

**Section 4: Career Path Ambiguity**

1. Have you ever felt uncertain or unclear about your next steps in terms of professional development? If yes:

* What specific factors contributed to this uncertainty?
	+ (Open-ended text field for respondents)
2a) How often do I feel that my organization's expectations and goals align with mine?

(Scale: Very Often, Somewhat Frequently, Rarely)

**Section 5: Additional Comments**

Is there anything else you'd like us know about your experiences or suggestions on how to improve career path clarity within our company? (Open-ended text field for respondents' feedback).

**Employee Motivation Survey**

As part of our ongoing efforts to understand what drives you and how we can best support your growth, please take this moment to share with us some insights about yourself. Your input will help shape initiatives that foster engagement, productivity, and overall job satisfaction.

1. **What motivates me at work:**
a) Recognition for my achievements
b) Opportunities for professional development & learning new skills 
c) Sense of accomplishment in completing tasks efficiently  
d) Collaborative environment with supportive colleagues   
e) Autonomy to make decisions independently    
f) Other (please specify): _______________________

2. **What are the most important factors that influence your job satisfaction?**
a) Clear goals and expectations from my manager
b) Meaningful work aligning with company values & mission 
c) Positive relationships within teams   
d) Opportunities for growth, promotions or new challenges  
e) Competitive compensation package    
f) Other (please specify): _______________________

3. **How often do you feel:**
a) Energized and motivated to tackle tasks
b) Neutral - just going through the motions
c) Frustrated with lack of resources/support   
d) Overwhelmed by workload or responsibilities  
e) Underutilizing my skills/talents    
f) Other (please specify): _______________________

4. **What would make you feel more engaged and motivated at work?**
a) More autonomy in decision-making
b) Regular feedback & coaching from manager 
c) Opportunities to take on new projects/initiatives   
d) Recognition for my contributions beyond just performance reviews  
e) Improved communication channels within teams    
f) Other (please specify): _______________________

5. **How do you currently prioritize your work?**

d) High workload/stress levels affecting productivity    
e) Other (please specify): _______________________

7. **How do you envision your ideal work environment:**

(Please provide any additional comments or suggestions that might help us better understand what drives and motivates our employees)

Thank You!

**Section 5: Overall Performance**

**Feedback Mechanics Questionnaire**

* Daily
* Weekly 
* Monthly

e.) None

Somewhat Important

	* Direct Reports

b. Quarterly or bi-annual performance reviews
c. Anonymous online surveys (e.g., this questionnaire)

	* Performance and progress towards goals?
	* Contributions/ideas/initiatives?

(Please select one or more)

b) Weekly/Month-to-month 
c) Quarterly/Semiannually
d. Annually/Half-year

3.

	* Managers/Supervisors?
	* Peers/Coworker?

(Please select all that apply)

a. Specific, actionable suggestions for improvement
b. Recognition/Acknowledgment/Praise 
c. Constructive criticism with clear explanations and examples

	* What was the purpose of providing this feedback?

[LLM ANSWER]
Here's a sample questionnaire for investigating internal mobility opportunities within an organization:

**Internal Mobility Opportunity Questionnaire**

As part of our ongoing efforts to improve employee development and retention, we're interested in understanding your experiences with moving roles or departments internally. Your input will help us identify areas where improvements can be made.

Please answer the following questions honestly based on your current role(s) at [Company Name].

**Section 1: Current Role**

* What is my primary job title?
	+ _______________________________________________________
* How long have I been in this position? (approximate)
	+ _______________________________

**Section 2: Internal Mobility Experience**

Have you ever moved to a new role or department within [Company Name]?

Yes No

If yes, please describe the experience:

___________________________________________________________________________________________________________

What motivated me to move roles/departments?
(Select all that apply)

* New challenges and opportunities
* Career advancement goals
* Desire for change in work environment/ culture
* Other (please specify) _______________________________

**Section 3: Barriers or Challenges**

Have you ever encountered any barriers when considering moving internally?

Yes No

If yes, please describe the barrier(s):

___________________________________________________________________________________________________________

What do I think is preventing me from exploring internal mobility opportunities?
(Select all that apply)

* Lack of awareness about available roles
* Limited information on job requirements and expectations
* Fear or uncertainty around change/transition process
* Other (please specify) _______________________________

**Section 4: Support Systems**

Do you feel supported in your current role?

Yes No

If yes, what specific support systems have been helpful to me? 
(Select all that apply)

	+ Mentorship programs
    + Training and development opportunities
    + Feedback from supervisors/managers
    + Peer-to-peer learning networks
* Other (please specify) _______________________________

**Section 5: Recommendations**

What would make you more likely or interested in exploring internal mobility options?

(Open-ended question for respondents to provide suggestions)

___________________________________________________________________________________________________________

Thank You!

Your input is invaluable! If there's anything else we can do better, please let us know.

This questionnaire aims at understanding the current state of employee experiences with moving roles/departments internally. It covers aspects such as motivation behind internal mobility decisions and potential barriers or challenges faced during this process.

Here's a comprehensive questionnaire for investigating pressure at work:

**Pressure at Work Questionnaire**

The purpose of this survey is to understand and measure various aspects related to job-related pressures. Your honest responses will help us identify areas where we can improve the working environment.

Please answer these questions based on your experiences in our organization, considering both positive (e.g., motivation) as well as negative pressure sources:

**Section 1: Perceived Pressure**

* On a scale of 0-5, how often do you feel overwhelmed by work demands? 
	+ Not at all
    + Rarely (<25%)
    + Sometimes (~50%-75%)
    + Often (76% -90%)
    + Almost always (>91%)

How many hours per week are spent on tasks that exceed your capacity?

* Less than 2 hrs/week
* Between 3-5 hr/wk 
	+ More details: _______________________________________

**Section 2: Pressure Sources**

Which of the following pressure sources do you experience regularly? (Select all applicable)

    * Unrealistic deadlines or expectations from management/supervisors
        + How often does this happen?
            - Daily, several times a week/week/month

* High workload volume and lack of resources 
	+ What specific tasks are affected by the high load?

* Conflicting priorities among multiple projects/tasks 

How do you manage these pressures? (Select all applicable)

    * Prioritize most critical task(s)
        + How often is this necessary?
            - Daily, several times a week/week/month

* Delegate or reassign less important tasks
	+ What specific strategies have been effective?

**Section 3: Coping Mechanisms**

What coping mechanisms do you use to manage pressure at work? (Select all applicable)

    * Time management techniques 
        + Which ones are most helpful?
            - _______________________________________

* Communication with colleagues or supervisors

How often does this help alleviate pressures:

	+ Daily, several times a week/week/month
?

**Section 4: Impact on Well-being**

To what extent do you experience the following due to pressure at work? (Scale of Not At All =0-5)

    * Stress 
        + How has stress affected your overall well-being?
            - _______________________________________

* Burnout or exhaustion

How often have these feelings persisted for more than a few days?

	+ Daily, several times a week/week/month
*

**Section 4: Suggestions and Feedback**

What suggestions do you offer to reduce pressure at work? (Open-ended text field)

Any additional comments about your experiences with job-related pressures:

(Additional open-text fields or space provided for respondents' feedback)

[LLM ANSWER]
Here's a sample roadmap planing feedback questionnaire:

**Roadmap Planning Feedback Questionnaire**

We value your input in helping us refine our company-wide roadmaps and ensure we're aligned with business goals. Your honest opinions will help shape the direction of future initiatives.

Please take 5-7 minutes to complete this survey, sharing your thoughts on what worked well during roadmap planning sessions for [insert project/initiative name]. We appreciate any suggestions or ideas you may have!

**Section A: Overall Experience**

1. On a scale from (Very Satisfied) -3-(Not at All), how would rate the overall experience of participating in this year's roadmapping process?

2. What did we do well during roadmap planning that contributed to your positive feedback? Please share specific examples or anecdotes.

**Section B: Communication and Collaboration**

1. How effective was communication throughout the project, considering factors like regular updates, clear expectations, etc.? (Scale from 5-Not at All) -3-(Very Effective)

2a. Which team members/ stakeholders were most helpful in providing valuable insights during roadmap planning? Please list their names.

2b. Were there any specific individuals or teams that could have been more involved to improve the overall outcome?

**Section C: Content and Prioritization**

1. How well did we prioritize initiatives based on business goals, customer needs, etc.? (Scale from 5-Not at All) -3-(Very Well)

2a. Were there any specific roadmap items that you felt were missing or under-prioritized? If so, please describe.

**Section D: Suggestions and Ideas**

1. What new ideas would like to see incorporated into future roadmaps?

(Open-ended text field for respondents' suggestions.)

Please provide your thoughts on the following:

2a. Are there any specific pain points you'd love us address in our next roadmap iteration? If so, please describe.

**Section E: Closing**

1. Any additional comments or feedback about this year's roadmap planning process?

Thank You!

Your input is invaluable!

Here's a sample questionnaire for investigating employee perceptions towards training and development programs:

**Training & Development Program Questionnaire**

We value our employees' growth and want to understand your experiences with various learning opportunities. Your feedback will help us improve the effectiveness of these initiatives.

Please answer honestly, as all responses are anonymous unless you choose otherwise at the end of this survey.


1. **Overall Satisfaction**
How satisfied were you overall with training programs offered by [Company Name]?

a) Very Satisfied
b) Somewhat Saturated (Neutral)
c) Not Too Happy

2. What type(s) of trainings have been most beneficial to your job performance? Please select all that apply:

* Technical skills development 
	+ e.g., software, tools or equipment training
* Soft Skills Development  
    + e.g., communication, leadership, teamwork building workshops)
* Industry-specific knowledge updates (e.g. regulatory changes)    
* Leadership and management courses   
Other [please specify]

3. **Training Methods**
Which of the following methods do you prefer for learning new skills?

a) Instructor-led training sessions
b) Online tutorials or webinars 
c) On-the-job mentoring/coaching  
d) Self-paced e-learning modules (e.g., video, text-based)
f Other [please specify]

4. **Training Frequency**
How often would be ideal to receive trainings on new skills?

a) Daily/Weekly updates
b) Monthly sessions or workshops    
* Quarterly refresher courses   
c) Annually scheduled training events

5. What do you think is the most significant barrier preventing employees from fully utilizing available learning opportunities? Please select one:

	+ Lack of time (workload)
    + Limited access to technology/internet connectivity 
   * Unclear expectations about what skills are needed for career advancement
* Other [please specify]

d) No evaluation process in place

(Open-ended text field for respondents' suggestions)

**Additional Comments**

Is there anything else that comes up when thinking about Training & Development Programs at [Company Name]?

[LLM ANSWER]
Here's a comprehensive Questionnaire for Investigating Employee Perceptions towards their work-life balance:

**Work-Life Balance Survey**

As part of our ongoing efforts to understand and improve your overall well-being, we're interested in hearing about how you manage the demands between personal life (outside working hours) versus professional responsibilities. Your input will help us identify areas where adjustments can be made for a better quality-of-work-life balance.

**Section 1: Demographics**

Please provide some basic information to ensure accurate representation:

* Department/Team:
* Job Title/Roles held in the past year
* Years of service with our organization

---

Now, let's dive into your work and personal life experiences!

**Section 2: Work-Life Balance Perceptions (Scale from Strongly Agree [5] to Disagree [1])**

Please rate how often you experience each statement:

1. I feel overwhelmed by my workload during non-work hours.
	* SA(5) | A4| ND3| D21
2. My work schedule allows for sufficient time with family/friends outside of working hours (e.g., evenings, weekends).
	* 12345

---

**Section 3: Time Management and Flexibility**

1a.) How often do you find yourself checking or responding to emails/texts during non-work times?

SA(5) | A4| ND2| D11
b. Do your work hours allow for flexibility in scheduling appointments, errands, etc.? (Scale from 0-10)

---

**Section 3: Self-Care and Leisure Activities**

1a.) How often do you engage with hobbies or activities outside of professional life?

SA(5) | A4| ND2| D11
b. Do your work hours allow for sufficient time to pursue personal interests (e.g., exercise, reading)?

---

**Section 3: Support Systems and Communication Channels**

1a.) How often do you feel supported by colleagues or supervisors when dealing with workload pressures?

SA(5) | A4| ND2| D11
b. Are there adequate communication channels for reporting work-life balance concerns (e.g., HR, supervisor)?

---

**Section 3: Job Satisfaction and Stress**

1a.) How satisfied are you overall in your current role? 

(Scale from Very Satisfied [5] to Not at All Satisfied [-2])
b. On a scale of 0-10, how stressed do you feel about work-life balance?

c. Have there been any significant changes or events that have impacted your job satisfaction/stress levels (e.g., new role, family issues)?

---

**Section 4: Suggestions and Feedback**

What would improve the overall quality-of-worklife for our employees? Please share specific ideas:

* Open-ended text box

Thank you so much! Your input is invaluable in helping us create a better work environment.

Here's a comprehensive Questionnaire for Investigating Employee Perceptions towards their work-life balance:

**Work-Life Balance Survey**

As part of our ongoing efforts to understand and improve your overall well-being, we're interested in hearing about how you manage the demands between personal life (outside working hours) versus professional responsibilities. Your input will help us identify areas where adjustments can be made for a better quality-of-work-life balance.

**Section 1: Demographics**

Please provide some basic information to ensure accurate representation:

* Department/Team:
* Job Title/Roles held in the past year
* Years of service with our organization

---

Now, let's dive into your work and personal life experiences!

**Section 2: Work-Life Balance Perceptions (Scale from Strongly Agree [5] to Disagree [1])**

Please rate how often you experience each statement:

1. I feel overwhelmed by my workload during non-work hours.
	* SA(5) | A4| ND3| D21
2. My work schedule allows for sufficient time with family/friends outside of working hours (e.g., evenings, weekends).
	* 12345

---

**Section 3: Time Management and Flexibility**

1a.) How often do you find yourself checking or responding to emails/texts during non-work times?

SA(5) | A4| ND2| D11
b. Do your work hours allow for flexibility in scheduling appointments, errands, etc.? (Scale from 0-10)

---

**Section 3: Self-Care and Leisure Activities**

1a.) How often do you engage with hobbies or activities outside of professional life?

SA(5) | A4| ND2| D11
b. Do your work hours allow for sufficient time to pursue personal interests (e.g., exercise, reading)?

---

**Section 3: Support Systems and Communication Channels**

1a.) How often do you feel supported by colleagues or supervisors when dealing with workload pressures?

SA(5) | A4| ND2| D11
b. Are there adequate communication channels for reporting work-life balance concerns (e.g., HR, supervisor)?

---

**Section 3: Job Satisfaction and Stress**

1a.) How satisfied are you overall in your current role?

[LLM ANSWER]
Here's a comprehensive questionnaire for investigating workload management within an organization:

**Workload Management Questionnaire**

The purpose of this survey is to understand how employees manage their workloads, identify challenges and opportunities in the current process. Your honest feedback will help us improve our processes.

Please answer these questions based on your experiences at [Company Name].

1.
How would you rate your overall workload management experience?

a) Very effective
b) Somewhat effective 
c) Neutral  
d) Not very well managed

2.
What is the most common task or project that takes up a significant portion of my time? (Select all applicable)

• Meetings and discussions with colleagues/team members/manager(s)
• Task-oriented work, such as data entry/reporting
• Project-based tasks requiring research/planning/design 
Other: _______________________________________

3. How often do you feel overwhelmed by your workload?

a) Frequently  
b) Occasionally   
c) Rarely    
d) Never

4.
What are the top three factors that contribute to feeling overloaded? (Rank in order of importance)

• Unrealistic deadlines
• Insufficient resources/staffing 
Other: _______________________________________

5. How do you prioritize your tasks when faced with multiple competing demands?

a) By urgency and criticality  
b) Based on task complexity   
c) According to the level manager's expectations    
d) Other (please specify): ______________________________

6.
What strategies or tools have been most effective in helping manage workload? 

• Task management software/apps
• Prioritization frameworks/templates 
Other: _______________________________________

7. How often do you take breaks during your workday?

a) Daily, multiple times  
b) Several days a week   
c) Rarely    
d) Never

8.
What would be the most helpful change to improve workload management? 

(Open-ended question for respondents)

9.
How confident are you in being able to manage an increased or changed workload effectively?
(Scale: 1-5, where 
•   = Not at all
    •     = Somewhat  
        Other (please specify): ______________________________

10. Any additional comments about your experience with managing workloads?

(Open-ended question for respondents)

Thank you very much! Your input is invaluable in helping us understand and improve our workload management processes.

Please let me know if this meets the requirements or would like to make any changes before converting it into a specific format (e.g., Excel, Google Forms).
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Workload Management

**Workplace Culture Questionnaire**

We're interested in understanding what makes our company an amazing place to work! Your feedback will help us shape and improve the overall atmosphere, making it even more enjoyable and productive. Please take your time to answer these questions honestly.

1a) On average how would rate today's workplace culture on a scale of 0-10 (where 5 is neutral)?

Please select one:

* Very Poor
* Fairly Bad
Fair

2b) What do you think are the most important values that our company should prioritize to create an amazing work environment? Please choose up to three from below and add any additional suggestions.

Values:
Collaboration, Innovation, Respect for Diversity & Inclusion,
Open Communication Transparency Accountability Fun Work-Life Balance Flexibility
Other (please specify)

3c) How often do you feel valued by your colleagues?

* Always or Most of the Time: 5-10 times a week.
Sometimes. Occasionally when something significant happens.

Rarely Less than once every two weeks

4d) What are some things that make coming to work enjoyable for YOU? (Check all applicable)

Good relationships with coworkers
Sense of accomplishment and pride in my role or projects Feeling supported by management Opportunities for growth & development Fun team-building activities Recognition/ Rewards Celebrations/Pizza parties Other: _______________________

5e) Have you ever felt uncomfortable, excluded from a conversation/group activity due to your background (age/gender/race/etc.)? If yes:

* Yes
No

6f) How would rate the overall sense of trust within our team?

Please select one:
Very High Somewhat Trustworthy Neutral Not Very Much At All Little or No Confidence

[LLM ANSWER]
Here's a sample questionnaire for investigating workplace environment:

**Workplace Environmental Survey**

We value our employees' opinions and want to understand their experiences in creating an optimal work atmosphere at [Company Name]. Your input will help us identify areas of strength, opportunities for improvement, and inform decisions that support your well-being.

Please answer the following questions honestly. All responses are anonymous unless you choose otherwise (see instructions).

**Section 1: Overall Satisfaction**

* On a scale from 0 to 10, how satisfied would you rate our workplace environment? 
	+ Not at all satisfying
    + Somewhat unsatisfying
    + Neutral/average satisfaction level
    + Slightly more than average satisfactory experience
    + Very or extremely fulfilling

**Section 2: Workspace and Facilities**

* How comfortable do you feel in your workspace?
   - Extremely uncomfortable (e.g., poor lighting, inadequate seating)
	+ Somewhat discomforting 
     * Neutral/average comfort level  
      More satisfied with the space than not 

How would rate our office facilities? Please select one:
    + Excellent
  Good/Fairly good   
* Poor/Below average

**Section 3: Communication and Feedback**

Do you feel that your voice is heard in meetings or discussions?
   - Rarely/Almost never 
	+ Sometimes, but not consistently  
     * Most of the time/I'm usually listened to  

How often do receive constructive feedback on performance? Please select one:
    + Regular (e.g., quarterly)   
* Occasionally/Sporadically
  Never/Rarely

**Section 4: Work-Life Balance**

Do you feel that your work schedule and expectations align with personal needs?
   - Not at all aligned 
	+ Somewhat misaligned  
     * Neutral/average alignment level  

How often do take breaks or time off to recharge? Please select one:
    + Daily/Hourly
  Several times a week   
* Rarely/Never

**Section 5: Team and Collaboration**

Do you feel that your team is supportive of each other?
   - Not at all 
	+ Somewhat  
     * Neutral/average level  

How would rate the overall collaboration within our teams? Please select one:
    + Excellent
  Good/Fairly good   
* Poor/Below average

**Section 6: Additional Comments**

Is there anything you'd like to share about your workplace environment that wasn't covered in this survey?

Thank You for taking time!

Please note:

1. This questionnaire is designed anonymously, but if desired (e.g., HR or management), please indicate at the end of each section.
2. Please answer based on recent experiences and observations.

Let me know when you're ready to convert it into a specific format!

1.
How would rate overall satisfaction with my workplace environment?

a) Very Satisfied
b) Somewhat satisfied, but there's room for growth
c) Neutral (it is what it is)
d) Dissatisfying

• Collaboration and teamwork among colleagues 
• Availability of necessary resources/equipment  
• Comfortable workspace design/furniture
• Opportunities for growth/development within my role   
Other (please specify): _______________________

a) Most days I come to the office feeling enthusiastic and engaged 
b) Some weeks are better than others; it depends on projects/tasks

d) Almost never

______________________________________________________________________
5.

b) Some areas are better than others – it depends on the team/department
c) Noise/distracting factors can be overwhelming at times  
d) There is no clear policy or management

6. What do you think about our current lighting, temperature control (heating/cooling), and air quality?

a) Excellent; I'm comfortable all day long 
b) Good – some areas could use improvement
c) Fairly average/neutral

7.

d) Almost never

a) Exceptionally clean/maintained throughout

C Fair/average (no major issues)
D Poor/unacceptable levels

• Very Strong
Somewhat present but room for growth

[LLM ANSWER]
Here's a sample questionnaire for investigating workplace environment:

**Workplace Environmental Survey**

As we strive to create an optimal work atmosphere, I'd like you take this opportunity to share your thoughts and opinions about our current workspace. Your input will help us identify areas of improvement.

Please answer the questions honestly based on your experiences in [Company Name].

1.
How would rate overall satisfaction with my workplace environment?

a) Very Satisfied
b) Somewhat satisfied, but there's room for growth
c) Neutral (it is what it is)
d) Dissatisfying

2. What do you think are the most significant factors that contribute to a positive work atmosphere in our office? Please select up to 3:

• Collaboration and teamwork among colleagues 
• Availability of necessary resources/equipment  
• Comfortable workspace design/furniture
• Opportunities for growth/development within my role   
Other (please specify): _______________________

3. How often do you feel energized, motivated, or inspired at work?

a) Most days I come to the office feeling enthusiastic and engaged 
b) Some weeks are better than others; it depends on projects/tasks  
c) Rarely – usually when working with a specific team/project
d) Almost never

4. What changes would you like us make in our workspace environment? Please provide suggestions:

______________________________________________________________________
5.
How do we currently handle noise levels, distractions (e.g., meetings), and interruptions?

a) It's well-managed; I rarely feel disrupted 
b) Some areas are better than others – it depends on the team/department
c) Noise/distracting factors can be overwhelming at times  
d) There is no clear policy or management

6. What do you think about our current lighting, temperature control (heating/cooling), and air quality?

a) Excellent; I'm comfortable all day long 
b) Good – some areas could use improvement
c) Fairly average/neutral   
Dissatisfying/uncomfortable at times 

7.
How often are we encouraged to take breaks or engage in self-care activities during work hours? (e.g., meditation, stretching)

a) Regular reminders and opportunities for relaxation 
b) Some days I'm reminded; others not
c) Rarely – usually when feeling overwhelmed/stressed  
d) Almost never

8. What do you think about the overall cleanliness of our workspace?

a) Exceptionally clean/maintained throughout   
B Good, with some areas needing attention    
C Fair/average (no major issues)
D Poor/unacceptable levels 

9.
How would rate your sense of community and connection among colleagues? Do we have a strong team spirit or camaraderie in the office?
• Very Strong
Somewhat present but room for growth 
Neutral – it's okay, nothing special   
Not very/none at all

10. Any additional comments about our workplace environment that you'd like to share?

______________________________________________________________________

Thank your participants and appreciate their input!
